<Rating>4< /Rating>< review>
We really enjoyed the location of the unit.  Sunsets were great, surfers were entertaining to watch.  We used the kitchen every day for breakfast and lunch, we found it to be well equipped.  Furnishings were comfortable and didn't appear to be worn out.  I found the bed in the master bedroom to be very comfortable.  Bathrooms were great with plenty of towels.  Some odds and ends that we found were very nice like beach chairs, snorkel gear, and a beach umbrella (the umbrella was a mess and needs replaced).

On the negative side . . . 1) The lighting in the kitchen is either REALLY bright or off.  We replaced bulbs in the range hood so we could have a nightlight (both bulbs were burnt out).  2) The sliding shutters between the bedroom and living room were dirty -- badly needed dusting (or worse).  3) For the air conditioning to be effective in the unit, we had to keep sliding shutters open and a fan circulating the air.  We were expecting to be able to close the shutters to have some privacy in that bedroom but that made the air conditioning ineffective in the rest of the unit.  4) There were two fans in the unit but we were only able to get one to work.

Overall, we enjoyed the unit and if we choose to return to The Big Island we would definitely consider this unit again.</review>

We were very disappointed in the property The Birdhouse, and wonder what the owners would think, if they walked in and had to stay for a week based on the amenities listed.

There is no dishwasher, as listed. This left us immediately washing dishes to use, because who knows how "clean" the previous renters were.

There is no DVD player (that we could find) for either TV, as listed.

There is no garden/backyard, as listed (on property management website).

There is no fireplace, as listed. This compounded with the fact that the heater in the living area is "inoperable" and the space heaters provided were not capable of heating a room in December made it miserable. (Have you gone in and tried to heat the place at 4:00 in the afternoon, in December?) The heater in the bedroom does warm up the room, but is too noisy to leave on when resting or sleeping (if you want to hear the ocean, which you can, even with closed doors). We left heaters on all night and still woke up to a cold house.

The linens provided are sorely lacking. The bathroom towels have stains on them, as do the thin sheets in the bedroom. The pillowcases were absolutely covered with pills, on both sides. No one wants to lay their head down on that.

We were immediately invaded by ants in the kitchen. We bought and brought groceries for our 6 night stay and couldn't even use the kitchen. The knives provided were left out on the kitchen counter, and had to be washed before use. Every time. The "kitchenette prepared with everything needed to prepare delicious meals" consists of one pot, and one pan, some salt and pepper, and opened soy sauce.

Besides these misrepresentations, it should be made clear that the parking area is VERY muddy (after rains), and you'll track mud everywhere. Including back into your car. Also, there are many more steps than the photos show. We were not prepared for that, as our luggage for a week's stay was heavy.

We spent 6 hours driving to what we thought was going to be a peaceful and lovely Christmas, only to be faced with a total and complete misrepresentation that forced us to drive 6 hours home the next day. These accommodations could be so lovely with a heating system that works (even one of those fake electric fireplaces), decent linens, a better stocked kitchen, and no ants. You'll need to correct your listing for fireplace, DVD, garden/backyard, and dishwasher so other renters know exactly what they're paying for.< /review>

< Review>
Grand Welcome's modern, spacious and well appointed (there were so many towels, pillows, linens were available!) Mauna Lani Golf Villas Unit Q-22 perfectly accommodated our family's weekend getaway. The children adored the pool (it's not too cold, not too deep and expansive enough to not be crowded), the adults enjoyed the quiet serenity of the complex (quite unlike the sprawling, crowded nearby resorts which cost much more), and the fully equipped kitchen allowed us to self cater most of our meals comfortably and easily without needing to add things (like we often do).

Grand Welcome also provided a personal phone call from an on-island agent once the booking was made, and then followed up with a second arrival call to make sure everything was all right with the self check in process. I have used a dozen other booking agencies/platforms over the last decade, and this is the only company that reached out in this way...and twice. Very impressed, and highly recommend both this company, and this unit. A large family would find the loft particularly private, roomy and an ideal third bedroom! You won't regret booking this accommodation in such a gorgeous setting with so much to do (the private beach club is something you won't find anywhere else on island).</Review>

1. The 2nd installment was charge by Grand Welcome 45 days prior to due date of Nov. 24 and without notification, I found out through credit card statement.

<review>Our family stayed in Maui in July 2019 for our annual family trip. We rented a two bedroom condo for two weeks, which was within walking distance to the Shops at Wailea and, another plus, the condo had a view to the ocean. We were excited to see plenty of beach chairs and an ice chest available for our use and the size of our condo was perfect for our family of 4.

However, within the first 10 minutes of arriving we were quickly disappointed. First, we opened up the wooden curtains in the living room to see the ocean and several pieces of each curtain came off (this was report to Grand Welcome and they offered to address it). Second, the listing stated the unit had air conditioning (it did but only in the bedrooms); therefore, we hardly felt comfortable cooking, eating or sitting in the living room, even with multiple fans circulating the hot air (the weather during our stay was 88-90 degrees consistently). There were also metal shutters throughout the unit. It was hard to open and close a few of them - the turning mechanisms could probably use some WD-40 or require strong wrists/muscles to open).

Third, the kitchen was not as adequately equipped (I wish there were more pots; baking sheets and cupcake pans; a rice cooker; wooden cooking utensils - the plastic ones bent while stirring; and BBQ utensils) than other condos we had rented and several of the baking pans were rusted. Additionally, there was a foul odor coming from the sink and we used the disposal to try to get rid of the smell, but it seemed to make it worse.

Fourth, we found that not all the outlets in the unit worked and it was hard to fall asleep at night due to the AC window units blaring in our ears. Additionally, the bed frame on one of the beds stuck out so much that my husband and I constantly hit our shins on it throughout our stay.

Fifth, we had vacationers above us during our whole stay who woke up at 5:30 am every morning (no fault of Grand Welcome and/or owner - but renter beware), which meant we would then be up due to the heavy walking (or stomping, jumping and running) happening above us.

And lastly, the unit came with two umbrellas for the beach. They came in handy, but one of them was broken and because of that, it made it hard to get into the sand. We didn‚Äôt use the bodyboard as it looked like it was falling apart. There weren‚Äôt any sand toys (not a big deal for anyone not traveling with kids), but it would‚Äôve been nice not to have needed to buy some.

I honestly wished we had had a more pleasant and more comfortable stay, especially since we were there for so long. Unfortunately, I don‚Äôt think we will be returning to this unit and would not recommend it to anyone traveling during summer time due to how hot the unit was in the common areas.< /review><pics>None< /pics><Response>None< /Response>< gmap_id>

Studio:

1) One of the guests stepped on a piece of glass in the shower stall and cut her foot.
2) The bedroom and bathroom were dark because light bulbs were.
3) The shower was either cold of tepid.
4) The bathroom sink stopper got stuck in the closed position so we had to remove the stopper to prevent the sink from overflowing.
5) TV did not work.

Master bedroom:
1) Bedroom smelled like mildew.
2) Bathroom tiles had mold.
3) Missing a bathmat in the tub, and one guest almost slipped and fell. We had to use a towel in the tub for a bathmat.
4)  Only bathroom with hot water for showers, so all of the guests had use in the master bath if they wanted a hot shower.

2nd bedroom:
1) A noise sporadically emanated from the hall toilet, disturbing the sleep of guests in the 2nd bedroom.  (We have a recording of the noise).
2) The shower was either cold of tepid.
3) TV did not work, could not get reception.

Hall Bathroom:
Two guests got locked in the bathroom.  The guests simply closed the door and found it locked when they attempted to exit. The door could not be unlocked from the inside. They had to exit to the outside to get out of the bathroom.

The living room screens were not useful because they did not pull out easily and did not extend far enough to cover the open doors.

< review>
What can I say?  We had just an incredibly good time in the apartment. Location great, view amazing, furnishings perfect.  We did not want to leave.  Being on the second floor was great and even though there were folks next to us on the same level (but different building) it was very quiet at night.  We cooked and ate most of our meals in the condo -  why go out and spend a lot of money on so-so food when you have the best dining view in Kona?  We are somewhat "foodies" and were glad that there was an excellent grocery store very near the condo. Also some good take out places near by.  Movie theatre was also nice to have in walking distance.  Definitely, we will be back.

But a few suggestions (the reason for 4 stars rather than 5)

1. Our check-in material did not have the correct entry code for the main gate and we were just lucky to be able to follow another car in at night before the gate closed.  We got the code from a nice neighbor.

2.  The Wifi log in and password that you gave us did not work.  Luckily, we had a tech savvy person with us and he got the log in off the back of the router and then the password was default.  Log in was: MySpectrumWifi98-5G and password was fancystate539.  Also, we had a a problem watching Netflix movies - way too much buffering.  We finally gave up. We could watch with no problem on our smaller devices so it was not an issue with the strength of the signal.  I think you should take a look at the whole Wifi set up to be sure folks can stream videos.

3. The kitchen was very well equipped.  Only thing missing:  a good knife sharpener.< /review>

(Translated by Google) A family of four went to Kailua-Kona on the Big Island of Hawaii. I stayed at a condominium called Kailua Bay Resort # 3301, which was very reasonable but had enough facilities for a long term stay. In particular, we had equipment (parasols, snorkeling masks, fins, etc.) for playing in the sea, so we could use it for free. There were two bedrooms and two shower rooms (with toilets), so we could spend a relaxing time with a family of four. The kitchen also had cooking utensils and utensils, plates, forks and spoons.
The service of the condominium management company was also very good. When my wife accidentally broke the coffee maker and contacted the management company by email, the next day I received a new coffee maker and was very surprised. I was so impressed that I was notified that I didn't need any money to break the coffee maker!
There were Longs Drugs and TKA around the condominium, and there were also Ross Dress for Less and Macy's if you extended a little, so it was a very convenient place.
I want to use it again when I go to the Big Island with my family!

< text>
This place has great tacos. They're small, but really tasty. They are open 24 hours a day (at least the drive-thru is). The parking lot is a bit small, but if you go when they're not busy, then you shouldn't have issues with parking. I had 3 tacos (I tend to go a bit non-traditional, so bear with me). I had one tongue taco, one head taco, and one tripas (intestines) taco. They have the regular carne asada, carnitas, chicken, etc. as well. They have burritos, quesadillas, and similar items, but their main thing is the tacos. Bathrooms are clean, too. :)< /text>

<rate>1</rate>< review>
Since moving to High Country Villas in March of 2016, my wife and I have experienced a couple of disturbing Encinitas mail carrier-related incidents.
We have had our outgoing mail dropped in the middle of the street by a young male carrier with no satchel. I found three OF MY OUTGOING letters in the street in front of my neighbor's house. When I saw the carrier was just across the street still doing deliveries, I asked him where was his satchel? He said he didn't have one. When I asked how my outgoing mail, which I was now holding, came to be lying in the middle of the street, that carrier said: "oh wow, those must have fallen out of my pocket. Sorry." I originally reported this to Carrie Mannon. This young carrier's apathy and disrespect was blatant, and he didn't seem to care, or at all proud to be a USPS carrier. What happened to the pride of the mail service?
Next, an orange "Beware of Dog" warning form (PS Form 1778) was found BY ME in the middle of MY street while on a random walk with my dog, ironically. Apparently, Edgar had dropped it "by mistake". It had MY home address on it and claimed that "We had a large dog that charged." IF THE HOMEOWNER ASSOCIATION GOT A HOLD OF THIS INFORMATION IT MIGHT BE GROUNDS FOR A FINE OR EVEN EVICTION. No one in my neighborhood is allowed to have a large, ill-tempered dog. And we don't. We have a 48-pound, 10-year old female Border Collie who is an extremely well-behaved service animal. I also reported this incident to Carrie Mannon. Edgar, who was the carrier in this incident, displayed a profound apathy, and "who cares" attitude...it was really disappointing. And Ms. Mannon was less than sympathetic listening to my complaint about the mishap!! She went silent in the middle of the conversation, and it was obvious she couldn't wait to hang up, and she could care less as well.
Finally, I phoned today to report another younger USPS carrier on my street with no satchel. He said his name was Happi, and that he forgot his satchel. Happi was here for the first time from Vista, filling in for the day, and had no experience with this route. I was told by Carrie Mannon when I phoned on the two prior occasions, that it was USPS policy that carriers wear a satchel to deliver the mail, to prevent all types of mistakes from happening, especially with new and junior carriers. Today Carrie seemingly changed policy, and said since "it was a light mail day; no one had to wear their satchels."

Are we the only postal customers enduring weird things with the Encinitas mail service??

Ms. Mannon next asked me if I had any outgoing mail today OR had I had an incident today. Both answers were "no". She then went on to say: "well, if nothing bad has happened today, why are you even calling me (AKA why are you bothering me)?

All I really wanted from Ms. Mannon was for her to clarify the policy on USPS carriers using satchels to keep mistakes from continuing to happen. So around and around she went, and took me on some confusing story about the use of satchels. Basically, NO ANSWER!
So here is a list of the social skills Supervisor Carrie Mannon displayed during our phone conversation on September 2, 2016:  argumentative, apathetic, unapologetic, condescending, and impatient. Carrie Mannon does NOT demonstrate the attributes of a USPS worker, let alone a supervisor!

I need to send a shout out to the new San Diego Postmaster Andre, the genius I met yesterday in his car while he was observing and following Raquel (Rockie), an OUTSTANDING CARRIER with nearly 30 years of mail carrier service, as if she were a rookie. Andre, the one who hired Carrie Mannon, had absolutely NO time for me to talk about Carrie Mannon while he was at a full stop, doing his observations. He chose to roll up his window in my face, mid-sentence, instead of listening to feedback regarding the Encinitas Garden View USPS facility supervision staff, specifically Carrie.
Great customer service, USPS. Way to go, Andre...you're as incompetent as your facility supervisor!< /review>

< Review>
I have patronized many Chipotle Mexican Grill branches over the last few years at various States and have always received consistent good services from these branches. However, on both occasions that I have visited the branch located at 4180 N 1st St UNIT 60, San Jose, CA 95134, the services that I had received are so bad that I decided to write a review about this branch. On my first visit about 3 weeks ago while waiting in queue, after serving the person in front of me, the female server suddenly decided that she wanted to work on some phone order and thus I have to wait for 5 minutes while she was working on this phone order. Now, there were at least 3 - 4 servers at the counter working on phone orders etc. but somehow this server decided to stop serving me and join the other servers as well after she had served at least 3 queuing customers who are in front of me without having them to wait. Nevertheless, I waited patiently for about 4-5 mins while she completed the phone order and then switched back to taking my in-person order.

On my second visit which was today 04/21/21 at around 6:00 pm, there was no customer in this branch when I went in to place my in-person order. However, although one female server (she subsequently claimed that she is the manager and her name is Melissa) and two other male servers were present at the counter, the female manager just walked away after noticing me and one of the male server also started moving between the counter and the kitchen while not really doing any work but just refusing to serve me. Thus, I had to wait for a few minutes before the 3rd server who was busily preparing for a phone order to tell me that he will start taking my order soon. After waiting for a few more minutes with no server willing to take my order (the second server still pretended to act busy by checking on the food packed by the third server), I informed the third server that they are providing very poor service to me by refusing to take my order. As such, I demanded to talk to the manager. However, instead of the manager coming to listen to my complaint, she sent a third male server to try to pacify me. When I realized that this third male server was not the manager and demanded to talk to the manager, she then reluctantly appeared with a defiant and unpleasant look in her face. She also claimed that all of them are busily handling phone orders and thus none of them are able to serve the only customer (myself) in the branch and thus she does not think that it is an issue if I had to wait for almost 10 minutes without anyone taking my order. Upon asking her name, she also initially tried to evade this question by providing some nonsensical replies before she eventually provided her first name as Melissa.
